//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table ACCSERIESRULES : Accessory series exclusion(...) rules
//
//		Rules:
//			ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID	// ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//			ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID	// ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//			>ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is built-in
//			^ACXXXID			// ACXXXID excludes all others
//		    *ACXXXID			// ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			#ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//			+ACXXXID 			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//			++ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
//
//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// Accesseories group for TA-COMPACT-P
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// TA-Modulator DN15 to DN50 have exactly the same body AND thread male connection for standard, international and US version.
// The international version has the same article number as the standard. Except for the connection accessories. 
// For standard version, we have only thread, for US version we have thread NPT and for international version we have both thread and thread NPT.
// By default we put all the connection accessories. It's the filter tab that will manage which accessories will be visible or not in regards to
// the current country.

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCGR_MODULATOR_15) -> PICVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"TA-Modulator 15"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}		// Specific for Modulator 15 male thread
	*ACCXFTH_15 \ !ACCXMTH_15 \ !ACCXW_15 \ !ACCXS_15 \ !ACCXS_16 \ !ACCXSE_15 \ !ACCXCMP_615 \ !ACCXCMP_618 \ !ACCXCMP_622 \ !ACCXFTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXMTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXSNPT_15      // 52163-015: With female thread
	*ACCXMTH_15 \ !ACCXFTH_15 \ !ACCXW_15 \ !ACCXS_15 \ !ACCXS_16 \ !ACCXSE_15 \ !ACCXCMP_615 \ !ACCXCMP_618 \ !ACCXCMP_622 \ !ACCXFTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXMTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXSNPT_15      // 0601-02.350: With male thread
	*ACCXW_15 \ !ACCXFTH_15 \ !ACCXMTH_15 \ !ACCXS_15 \ !ACCXS_16 \ !ACCXSE_15 \ !ACCXCMP_615 \ !ACCXCMP_618 \ !ACCXCMP_622 \ !ACCXFTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXMTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXSNPT_15      // 52009-015: Welding connection
	*ACCXS_15 \ !ACCXFTH_15 \ !ACCXMTH_15 \ !ACCXW_15 \ !ACCXS_16 \ !ACCXSE_15 \ !ACCXCMP_615 \ !ACCXCMP_618 \ !ACCXCMP_622 \ !ACCXFTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXMTHNPT_15 \ !ACCXSNPT_15      // 52009-515: Soldering connection on pipe 15

	// HYS-2031
	// In the database to manage a particular case of excluded products we do as follow:
	//   * In Cv accessory table (CDB_RuledTable where stem heater is listed),
	//     in the accessory line, we add exlusion sign before adding excluded product.
	//     Stem heater \ !Adapter.
	//    
	//   * In actuator adapter table(CDB_RuledTable where the adapter is listed),
	//     in the adapter line, we add exclusion sign before adding excluded product.
	//     Adapter \ !Stem heater
	// 
	// We look the two tables to manage exclusion
	// /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table VALVE_CHAR_TAB : Table of regulating valve characteristics
//
//	new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(ID\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//			Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//			SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//		}
//		Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//		Min recommended setting (for selection)
//		Number of curves: 1 = Kv catalogue only; 4 = Kv catalogue, Lambda, Re* and Kv from test.
//		opening 1 \ Kv 1
//		opening 2 \ Kv 2
//		...
//	}
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_ValveCharacteristic(C_TBV-C15\1) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
{
	{
		#eDISCRETE_False									// #eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
		#eTURN_Single                                       // #eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
		0.25												// Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
	}
	1.0													// Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
	3.0                                                 // Min recommended setting (for selection)
	1                                                   // Number of curves: 0 = no curve; 1 = Kv catalogue only; 4 = Kv catalogue, Lambda, Re* and Kv from test.
	0.00 \ 0.00                                         // opening 1 \ Kv 1
	1.00 \ 0.09
	2.00 \ 0.26
	3.00 \ 0.53
	4.00 \ 0.78
	5.00 \ 0.99
	6.00 \ 1.23
	7.00 \ 1.43
	8.00 \ 1.59
	9.00 \ 1.71
	10.0 \ 1.80
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
// Pressure independent valve characteristics
//
//  new:CDB_PICVCharacteristic(ID) -> VALVE_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				Discrete/Continuous: 				#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined
//				Single/Multi/Electronic-turn: 		#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined
//				SettingRounding						Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//			}
//			Min measurable setting (for TA-Scope)
//			Min recommended setting (for selection)
//			Number of curves: 1 = Kv catalogue only; 4 = Kv catalogue, Lambda, Re* and Kv from test.
//			Opening 1 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			Opening 2 \ Kv catalogue [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			...
//		}
//		Kvd				Kvs of the Dp controller
//		Fc				Stabilized Dp in the throttle
//		Qmax			Max flow of the valve
//		Number of curves: 0 = no curve; 1 = Qmax curve; 2 = Qmax and Dpmin curve; 3 = Stroke
//		Setting 1 \ qmax 1 \ Dpmin 1 \ Stroke 1
//		Setting 2 \ qmax 2 \ Dpmin 2 \ Stroke 2
//		...
//	}
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// TA-MODULATOR
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_Curve
//
//	Inherite from CData
//
//	new:CDB_Curve(ID)->tableID
//	{
//		n				// Number of functions associated to the abscissa.
//		x0 \ y0			// Points X0\Y0(0)\...\Y0(n-1) DpL \ +-% of deviation
//		x1 \ y1
//		...
//	}
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// These three following curves describe the Dpk in regards to the flow.
// DpK is the differential pressure that the DP-controller stabilize (equals the differential pressure over
// the TA-COMPACT-DP control part and the load).
new:CDB_Curve(DPCBCV_QDPK_10\1)->DPC_CHAR_TAB
{
	1													// Number of functions associated to the abscissa.
	2.638888888889E-05 \ 1.514641817175E+04  			// Points X0\Y0(0)\...\Y0(n-1) DpL \ +-% of deviation
	2.500000000000E-05 \ 1.527842231051E+04
	2.361111111111E-05 \ 1.541855709153E+04
	2.222222222222E-05 \ 1.556028062665E+04
	2.083333333333E-05 \ 1.573581671358E+04
	1.944444444444E-05 \ 1.592451906102E+04
	1.805555555556E-05 \ 1.610733341528E+04
	1.666666666667E-05 \ 1.628622244076E+04
	1.527777777778E-05 \ 1.646511146623E+04
	1.388888888889E-05 \ 1.677124955432E+04
	1.250000000000E-05 \ 1.710821762893E+04
	1.111111111111E-05 \ 1.744970668834E+04
	9.722222222222E-06 \ 1.782038957593E+04
	8.333333333333E-06 \ 1.819107246353E+04
	6.944444444444E-06 \ 1.856175535112E+04
	5.555555555556E-06 \ 1.902378303013E+04
	4.166666666667E-06 \ 1.950001086299E+04

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	DpC BCV characteristics
//
//	Remark: - It's typically for valve with combined Dp-controller valve and a balancing & control valve (i.e: TA-COMPACT-DP)
//          - See remark in the 'CDB_ValveCharacteristic' for the difference between Kvsignal and Kv.
//          - Here the CDB_ValveCharacteristic part contains Kvsignal for measure in TA-Scope.
//
//
//	new:CDB_DpCBCVCharacteristic(ID) -> DPCBCV_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				Discrete/Continuous enum				Discrete set of data or continuous characteristic (#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined).
//				Single/Multi/Electronic-turn			Number of turns of the valve (#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined).
//				SettingRounding							Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
//			}
//			Min measurable setting (For TA-Scope)
//			Min recommended setting (for selection)
//			Number of curves
//			Opening 1 \ Kvsignal [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			Opening 2 \ Kvsignal [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
//			...
//		}
//		Kvm						max Kv of the DP-controller in the valve (control part excluded).
//		Qmin					Min flow of the valve.
//		Qmax					Max flow of the valve.
//		Dplmin					Minimum Dp that can be stabilized.
//		FlowDeltaPkCurveID		Stabilized Dp characteristic (curve with relation between the flow and Dpk).
//								'Dpk' is the Dp stabilized from the internal point of the valve between the Dp-controller and the control part to
//                              the point after the load.
//		SettingKvcCurveID		Kvc characteristic (curve with relation between setting and Kvc,D).
//								'c' because it concerns the control part of the valve and 'D' for design.
//	}
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
// TA-COMPACT-DP
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
new:CDB_DpCBCVCharacteristic(C_COMPACT_DP10\1) -> DPCBCV_CHAR_TAB
{
	{
		{
			#eDISCRETE_False				// Discrete set of data or continuous characteristic (#eDISCRETE_True, #eDISCRETE_False or #eDISCRETE_Undefined).
			#eTURN_Single                   // Number of turns of the valve (#eTURN_Single, #eTURN_Multi, #eTURN_Electronic or #eTURN_Undefined).
			0.25							// Allows to know how to round the result of a computing setting.
		}
		1.0								// Min measurable setting (For TA-Scope)
		3.0                             // Min recommended setting (for selection)
		1                               // Number of curves: 1 = Kv catalogue only; 4 = Kv catalogue, Lambda, Re* and Kv from test.
		0.00 \ 0.000                    // Opening 1 \ Kvsignal [ \ Lambda \Re* \ Kv from test ]
		1.00 \ 0.0535
		2.00 \ 0.0975
		3.00 \ 0.133
		4.00 \ 0.170
		5.00 \ 0.199
		6.00 \ 0.228
		7.00 \ 0.249
		8.00 \ 0.269
		9.00 \ 0.283
		10.0 \ 0.297
	}
	1.75							// Kvm: max Kv of the DP-controller in the valve (control part excluded).
	2.500000000E-06					// Qmin
	2.583333334E-05					// Qmax
	5000							// Dplmin
	DPCBCV_QDPK_10					// FlowDeltaPkCurveID
	DPCBCV_KVCSET_10				// SettingKvcCurveID
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	How to write a control valve information ?
//	---------------------------------------------
//
//	new:CDB_ControlValve(ID)->BALCTRLVALV_TAB
//	{
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							0				isDeleted
//							1				isAvailable
//							0				isHidden
//							1				isFix
//							0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
//							0				Free integer
//      					0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//						}
//						Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//						PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//						Tmax in C
//						Tmin in C
//					}
//					"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//					"Name"					Name of the product
//					TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//					FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//					VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//					PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//					Comment					Product comment
//					ProdImgID				Product image ID
//					AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//					PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//					TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//					Price					Price of the product
// 					ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//					AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//					isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   				AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//					AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//				}
//				BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//				SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//				ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//				ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//				Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//				CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//				CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//				CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//				CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//				CBIVersion				CBI Version
//				Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//				MeasPt					Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//				MeasurableData			Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//				InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//				OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//			}
//			CharactID		Identifier of the valve characteristic
//		}
//		Kvs					Kvs of the CV
//		Stroke				Stroke of the CV
//		Rangeability		Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
//		LeakageRate			Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//		CloseOffCharID		Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//		ActuatorGroupID		Identifier of the actuator group
//		CvAdapterGroupID	Identifier of the CV adapter group
//		CtrlPropID			Identifier of the control properties
//		AdapterListMode		Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//							(see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//	CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//	CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//	CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//	CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//	CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//	CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//	CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

/////////////////
// *** TBV-C ****
/////////////////

new:CDB_ControlValve(TBV-C15LFA_TV\1) -> BALCTRLVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					{
						0													// isDeleted
						1                                                   // isAvailable
						0                                                   // isHidden
						1                                                   // isFix
						1                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
						0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
						0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
					}
					0.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6										// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
					NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
					120.0                                               // Tmax in C
					-20.0                                               // Tmin in C
				}
				"52133-015"											// Reference to the TA Product
				"TBV-C 15LF"                                        // Name of the product
				RVTYPE_BVC                                          // Identifier of the valve type
				FAM_TBV-C                                           // Identifier of the family of the product
				VERS_STD                                            // Identifier of the version of the product
				1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
				""                                                  // Product comment
				"PX_TBV-C20"                                        // Product image ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the accessory group
				#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
				NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
				0.0                                                 // Price of the product
				#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
				0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
				NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
				NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
			}
			BDY_AMETAL											// Identifier of the body material
			DN_15                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
			CONN_THREADM                                        // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
			NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
			NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
			"TBV-C"                                             // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
			"15LF"                                              // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
			"1/2LF"                                             // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
			1                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
			"4A"                                                // CBI Version
			1.0e+5                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
			#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointOutlet                // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
			#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpAvail   // Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
			NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
			NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
		}
		C_TBV-C15LF											// Identifier of the valve characteristic
	}
	0.90												// Kvs of the CV
	4.0e-3		                						// Stroke of the CV
	0.0			                						// Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
	0.0			                						// Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
	COC_TBV-C15	                						// Identifier of the close-off characteristic
	ACTGR_TBV_C	                						// Identifier of the actuator group
	NO_ID		                						// Identifier of the CV adapter group
	CP_TBV-C	                						// Identifier of the control properties
	#eCVAdapterListNA           						// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
                                						// (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table PICTRLVALV_TAB : Pressure independent ctrl valves
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_PIControlValve(ID)->PICTRLVALV_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							{
//								0				isDeleted
//								1				isAvailable
//								0				isHidden
//								1				isFix
//								0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//								0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//      						0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//							}
//							Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//							PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//							Tmax in C
//							Tmin in C
//						}
//						"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//						"Name"					Name of the product
//						TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//						FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//						VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//						PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//						Comment					Product comment
//						ProdImgID				Product image ID
//						AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//						PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//						TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//						Price					Price of the product
// 						ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//						AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//						isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   					AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//						AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//					}
//					BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//					SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//					ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//					ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//					Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//					CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//					CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//					CBIVersion				CBI Version
//					Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//					MeasPt					Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//					MeasurableData			Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//					InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//					OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//				}
//				CharactID				// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in PICVCharID
//			}
//			Kvs						Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
//			Stroke					Stroke of the CV
//			Rangeability			Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
//			LeakageRate				Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//			CloseOffCharID			Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//			ActuatorGroupID			Identifier of the actuator group
//			CvAdapterGroupID		Identifier of the CV adapter group
// 			CtrlPropID				Identifier of the control properties
//			AdapterListMode			Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//									(see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//		}
//		PICVCharID		Identifier of the PICV characteristic
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//  CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//	CDB_TAProduct::BodyMaterialID
//	CDB_TAProduct::SizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnectID
//	CDB_TAProduct::ConnTabID
//	CDB_TAProduct::Conn2ID
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIType
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISize
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBISizeInch
//  CDB_TAProduct::CBICompatibilityIndex
//	CDB_TAProduct::CBIVersion
//	CDB_TAProduct::Dpmax
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasPt
//	CDB_TAProduct::MeasurableData
//	CDB_TAProduct::InletSizeID
//	CDB_TAProduct::OutletSizeID
//	CDB_RegulatingValve::CharactID
//	CDB_ControlValve::Kvs
//	CDB_ControlValve::Stroke
//	CDB_ControlValve::Rangeability
//	CDB_ControlValve::LeakageRate
//	CDB_ControlValve::CloseOffCharID
//	CDB_ControlValve::ActuatorGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CvAdapterGroupID
//	CDB_ControlValve::CtrlPropID
//	CDB_ControlValve::AdapterListMode
//  CDB_PIControlValve::PICVCharID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//////////////////////////////
// Male Thread
//////////////////////////////

// *** TA MODULATOR *** //
//////////////////////////

// Standard and international version.
new:CDB_PIControlValve(TA_MODULATOR_15A\1) -> PICTRLVALV_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				{
					{
						{
							0													// isDeleted
							1                                                   // isAvailable
							0                                                   // isHidden
							1                                                   // isFix
							1                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
							0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						1.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6  									// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						90.0                                                // Tmax in C
						-10.0                                               // Tmin in C
					}
					"52164-315"											// Reference to the TA Product
					"TA-Modulator 15"                          			// Name of the product
					PICVTYPE_STD                               			// Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_MODULATOR_P                            			// Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_STD                                   			// Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                          			// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                         			// Product comment
					"PX_COMPACTP_15"                           			// Product image ID
					ACCGR_MODULATOR_15                        			// Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                             			// Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                        			// Price of the product
					#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
				}
				BDY_AMETAL											// Identifier of the body material
				DN_15                                       		// Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_THREADM                                		// Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                       		// Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                       		// Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				"TA-COMPACT-P"                              		// Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"15"                                        		// Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"1/2N"                                      		// Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				1                                           		// CBI compatibility Index
				"5L"									            // CBI Version (5L -> Doesn't exist to allow to get it in TA-Scope but not in CBI)
				4e+5                                        		// Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut   		// Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpStab | #eMeasDataDpAvail | #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn	// Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID												// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in PICVCharID
		}
		1.426												// Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
		4.02e-3                                             // Stroke of the CV
		">75"                                               // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
		1e-4                                                // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		COC_MODULATOR_P1520                                 // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_MODULATOR_P1520                               // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_MODULATOR-P                                      // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA									// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
		                                                	// (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	CPICV_MODULATOR_P15									// Identifier of the PICV characteristic
}

							1                                                   // isAvailable

							1                                                   // isFix
							1                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
							0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						0.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                     // Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						90.0                                                // Tmax in C
						-10.0                                               // Tmin in C
					}
					"52164-010"											// Reference to the TA Product
					"TA-Compact-P 10"                                   // Name of the product
					PICVTYPE_STD                                        // Identifier of the valve type
					FAM_COMPACT_P                                       // Identifier of the family of the product
					VERS_STD                                            // Identifier of the version of the product
					1                                                   // Level of priority for selection [1,10]
					""                                                  // Product comment
					"PX_COMPACTP_15"                                    // Product image ID
					ACCGR_COMPACT_P10                                   // Identifier of the accessory group
					#ePartOfaSetNo                                      // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
					0.0                                                 // Price of the product
					#eProduct                              	            // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
					0                                                   // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
				}
				BDY_AMETAL											// Identifier of the body material
				DN_10                                               // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_THREADM                                        // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				"TA-COMPACT-P"                                      // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"10"                                                // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"3/8N"                                              // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				1                                                   // CBI compatibility Index
				"5J"                                                // CBI Version
				4.0e+5                                              // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut           // Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpStab | #eMeasDataDpAvail | #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn 	// Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID												// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in PICVCharID
		}
		0.291												// Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
		4.0e-3                                              // Stroke of the CV
		">50"                                               // Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
		1e-4                                                // Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		COC_COMPACT_P1020                                   // Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_COMPACT_P10                                   // Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_COMPACT-P                                        // Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA									// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
		                                                    // (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}
	CPICV_COMPACT_P10									// Identifier of the PICV characteristic
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		CDB_DpCBCValve : Dp-Controller and Balancing control valve.
//      Ex: TA-COMPACT-DP
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_DpCBCValve(ID)->DPCBALCTRLVALV_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						{
//							{
//								0				isDeleted
//								1				isAvailable
//								0				isHidden
//								1				isFix
//								0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
//								0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//      						0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//							}
//							Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//							PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//							Tmax in C
//							Tmin in C
//						}
//						"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//						"Name"					Name of the product
//						TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//						FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//						VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//						PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//						Comment					Product comment
//						ProdImgID				Product image ID
//						AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//						PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
//						TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//						Price					Price of the product
// 						ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//						AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//						isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   					AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//						AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//					}
//					BodyMaterialID			Identifier of the body material
//					SizeID					Identifier of the corresp. valve size
//					ConnectID				Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
//					ConnTabID				Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
//					Conn2ID					Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
//					CBIType					Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISize					Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
//					CBISizeInch				Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
//					CBICompatibilityIndex	CBI compatibility Index
//					CBIVersion				CBI Version
//					Dpmax					Maximum Dp of the valve
//					MeasPt					Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
//					MeasurableData			Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
//					InletSizeID				Identifier of the inlet size ID
//					OutletSizeID			Identifier of the outlet size ID
//				}
//				CharactID				// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in DPCBCVCharID
//			}
//			Kvs						Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
//			Stroke					Stroke of the CV
//			Rangeability			Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
//			LeakageRate				Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
//			CloseOffCharID			Identifier of the close-off characteristic
//			ActuatorGroupID			Identifier of the actuator group
//			CvAdapterGroupID		Identifier of the CV adapter group
// 			CtrlPropID				Identifier of the control properties
//			AdapterListMode			Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
//									(see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
//		}
//		DPCBCVCharID		Identifier of the DPCBCV characteristic
//	}
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

							0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
						}
						0.6e+6 \ 1.6e+6                                 	// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
						NO_ID                                               // PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
						120.0                                               // Tmax in C
						-20.0                                               // Tmin in C
					}
					"52164-210"							                // Reference to the TA Product
					"TA-Compact-DP 10"					                // Name of the product

					FAM_COMPACT_DP						                // Identifier of the family of the product

					#ePartOfaSetNo						                // Boolean indicating if product is part of a set. Can be #ePartOfaSetNo, #ePartOfaSetYes, #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOk or #ePartOfaSetYesBreakOnMsg.
					NO_ID												// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.

					NO_ID                                               // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)

					NO_ID                                      	        // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
					NO_ID										        // Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
				}
				BDY_AMETAL								            // Identifier of the body material
				DN_10									            // Identifier of the corresp. valve size
				CONN_THREADM							            // Identifier of the (inlet/pipe side) connection
				NO_ID									            // Identifier of the connection table, can be NO_ID
				NO_ID									            // Identifier of the outlet/body side connection, can be NO_ID
				"TA-COMPACT-DP"							            // Type of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"10"									            // Size of the valve as used in the CBI II
				"3/8N"									            // Size of the valve in inch as used in the CBI II
				1										            // CBI compatibility Index
				"5L"									            // CBI Version (5L -> Doesn't exist to allow to get it in TA-Scope but not in CBI)
				4.0e+5									            // Maximum Dp of the valve
				#eMeasPointInlet | #eMeasPointMeasStatOut			// Measuring points. #eMeasPointNone or a combination of #eMeasPointInlet, #eMeasPointOutlet, #eMeasPointMeasStatOut or #eMeasPointP+.
				#eMeasDataDp | #eMeasDataFlow | #eMeasDataDpStab | #eMeasDataDpAvail | #eMeasDataDpSignal | #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn		// Measurable data. #eMeasDataNone or a combination of #eMeasDataDp, #eMeasDataFlow, #eMeasDataDpSignal, #eMeasDataDpAvail, #eMeasDataDpStab or #eMeasDataDpCAlwaysOn.
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the inlet size ID
				NO_ID												// Identifier of the outlet size ID
			}
			NO_ID												// MUST BE SET TO "NO_ID" -> valve characteristic is set now in DPCBCVCharID
		}
		0.29												// Kvs of the CV (Kvs is the Kv at full opening)
		4.0e-3												// Stroke of the CV
		">50"												// Rangeability of the CV, introduce as a double or as a string ">100" only '>' is supported
		1e-4												// Leakage rate of the CV as a fraction of Kvs
		COC_COMPACT_P1020									// !! Same as the TA-COMPACT-P - Identifier of the close-off characteristic
		ACTGR_COMPACT_P10									// !! Same as the TA-COMPACT-P - Identifier of the actuator group
		NO_ID												// Identifier of the CV adapter group
		CP_COMPACT-P										// Identifier of the control properties
		#eCVAdapterListNA									// Set what is the method to use to retrieve adapter list linked to this control valve (#eCVAdapterListNormal or #eCVAdapterListSpecial).
															// (see enum in 'tadb.txt' for more description).
	}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table PICVACCGROUP_TAB : Control valve accessory groups
//
//		Rules:
//			ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID	// ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//			ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID	// ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//			>ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is built-in
//			^ACXXXID			// ACXXXID excludes all others
//		    *ACXXXID			// ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			#ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//			+ACXXXID 			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//			++ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACBCVGR_FUSION_P3250) -> PICVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"TA-FUSION-P 32-50"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}
	*ACRV2
	++ACSTEMHEATER_32_50
}

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACBCVGR_FUSION_P32MT) -> PICVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"TA-FUSION-P 32 ISO228"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}		// Specific for FUSION-P 32 male thread
	*ACRV2
	*ACCXW_32 \ !ACCXS_32 \ !ACCXSE_32
	*ACCXS_32 \ !ACCXW_32 \ !ACCXSE_32
	*ACCXSE_32 \ !ACCXS_32 \ !ACCXW_32
	++ACSTEMHEATER_32_50
}

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACBCVGR_FUSION_P40MT) -> PICVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"TA-FUSION-P 40 ISO228"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}		// Specific for FUSION-P 40 male thread
	*ACRV2
	*ACCXW_40 \ !ACCXS_40 \ !ACCXSE_40
	*ACCXS_40 \ !ACCXW_40 \ !ACCXSE_40
	*ACCXSE_40 \ !ACCXS_40 \ !ACCXW_40
	++ACSTEMHEATER_32_50
}

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACBCVGR_FUSION_P50MT) -> PICVACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"TA-FUSION-P 50 ISO228"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}		// Specific for FUSION-P 50 male thread
	*ACRV2
	*ACCXW_50 \ !ACCXS_50 \ !ACCXSE_50
	*ACCXS_50 \ !ACCXW_50 \ !ACCXSE_50
	*ACCXSE_50 \ !ACCXS_50 \ !ACCXW_50
	++ACSTEMHEATER_32_50
}

{
	{
		"KTM 512 DN15-50 accessories"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}		
	++ACSTEMHEATER_15_50

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table PICVACTSET_TAB : Control valve/Actuator sets
// When reading CDB_Set object (txt file) TAS4 will update
// First and Second ID, TA_Product::PartOfASet member variable
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//	new:CDB_Set(ID)->PICVACTSET_TAB
//	{
//		{
//			0				isDeleted
//			1				isAvailable
//			0				isHidden
//			1				isFix
//			0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//			0				Free integer (bit 0: NotForIndSel, bit 1: NotForDirSel, bit 2: NotForHMCalc)
//      	0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//		}
//		"Reference"			Reference to the TA Product
//		"Name"				Name of the product
//		FirstID				Identifier of the control valve
//		SecondID			Identifier of the actuator
//		"Parameter"			String to allow to apply some filter.
//		"NextID"			Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
//	}
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//	CDB_Set::Reference
//	CDB_Set::Name
//	CDB_Set::FirstID
//	CDB_Set::SecondID
//	CDB_Set::AccGroupID
//	CDB_Set::Parameter
//	CDB_Set::NextID
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////


////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		ROOT TABLE identification
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

ROOT_TABLE(ROOT_TABLE)
